There are not too many “firsts” left for the Puppets to experience, but out of the blue, Curt was invited to meet with 1st, 2nd, and 3rd graders (!!) at Suder Montessori Magnet School in Chicago.\n\nSuder teacher Rachel Jacobson was the match maker:\n\n“I have put forth the idea that Curt Kirkwood is the coolest person that walks\nthe earth and my kids have bought in…showing up will confirm it all.”\n\nWhen the kids dropped a video along with the invite, https://splice.gopro.com/v?id=YpQbL5q1L, that did it, and the band got to cut loose with the kids singing along.\n\nTears were had.\n\nFollowing that outing, the band has started to revisit the folk and singer-song writer nuggets Curt put out in 2005 on his solo masterpiece, Snow, as well as similarly veined tracks from Rat
